help 2020-01-11 19:20:50 <@!282972760094015489> make sure your placement of wing panels and the mass centre are good
help 2020-01-11 19:21:34 with placement of wings, make sure the drag centre is in the middle
help 2020-01-11 19:21:42 same with mass
help 2020-01-11 19:22:15 also, to fix oversteering, get something to stabilize you mid-air
help 2020-01-11 20:49:27 ugh
help 2020-01-11 20:50:16 imagine the centre of mass as a point where if you put a stick below it on you vehicle, it would stay stable, wouldn't tip
help 2020-01-11 20:50:56 same with rockets, if your centre of mass is off the middle then the rocket starts tipping
help 2020-01-11 20:51:16 similar thing happens with the centre of drag
help 2020-01-11 20:51:44 when you move a thing, if the force you are applying isnt behind the centre of drag, the thing also starts tipping
help 2020-01-11 20:52:06 ugh, jsut google it
help 2020-01-11 20:52:10 as im bad at explaining
help 2020-01-11 20:52:34 the centre of mass or drag is just the average position of where either the mass is or the drag is
help 2020-01-11 20:53:02 similar, when you are flying upwards in your vtol, you need to have your centre of drag and mass in the middle or it will also start tipping
help 2020-01-11 20:55:14 <@!282972760094015489> it's a good idea to first know what those things are before you even start building a vtol

That's funny, that's a cool reference. But I kept going, I'd see a fridge that looked like among us, I'd see an animated bag of chips that looked like among us, I'd see a hat that looked like among us. And every time I'd burst into an insane, breath deprived laugh staring at the image as the words AMOGUS ran through my head. It's torment, psychological torture, I am being conditioned to laugh maniacly any time I see an oval on a red object. I can't fucking live like this... I can't I can't I can't I can't I can't! I could watch a man murder everyone I love and all I would be able to say is "red sus" and laugh like a fucking insane person. And the word "among" is ruined. The phrase "among us" is ruined. I can't live anymore. Among us has destroyed my fucking life. I want to eject myself from this plane of existence. MAKE IT STOP!
